anb_define_long_lived_heir = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { heirAge = $age$ }
		export_to_variable = {
			which = birthDate
			value = trigger_value:is_year
		}
		
		subtract_variable = {
			which = birthDate
			which = heirAge
		}
	}

											[[dynasty]dynasty=$dynasty$]
											[[religion]religion=$religion$]
											[[female]female=$female$]
											[[male]male=$male$]
											[[hidden]hidden=$hidden$]
										}
										
									}
									if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = birthDate value = 24 } } }
										define_heir = {
											birth_date = 20.1.1
											[[adm]adm=$adm$]
											[[dip]dip=$dip$]
											[[mil]mil=$mil$]
											[[max_random_adm]max_random_adm=$max_random_adm$]
											[[max_random_dip]max_random_dip=$max_random_dip$]
											[[max_random_mil]max_random_mil=$max_random_mil$]

											[[hidden]hidden=$hidden$]
										}
										
									}
								}
								if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = birthDate value = 20 } } }
									if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = birthDate value = 16 } }
										define_heir = {
											birth_date = 16.1.1
											[[adm]adm=$adm$]

											[[hidden]hidden=$hidden$]
										}

										define_heir = {

											[[dip]dip=$dip$]

									}
								}
							}
							if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = birthDate value = 12 } } }
								if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = birthDate value = 4 } }
									if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = birthDate value = 8 } }
										define_heir = {
											birth_date = 8.1.1
											[[adm]adm=$adm$]
											[[dip]dip=$dip$]

									if = { limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { which = birthDate value = 8 } } }
										define_heir = {
											birth_date = 4.1.1
											[[adm]adm=$adm$]

									define_heir = {
										birth_date = 0.1.1
										[[adm]adm=$adm$]
